    82	        /// <summary>
    83	        /// Gets the resource metadata, if this is a base resource type.
    84	        /// </summary>
    85	        internal ArmResourceMetadata? ResourceMetadata => _resourceMetadata;
    86	
    87	        /// <summary>
    88	        /// Gets the parent resource's CSharpType via the output library, or null for top-level resources.
    89	        /// </summary>
    90	        private CSharpType? ParentResourceType
    91	            => _resourceMetadata?.ParentResourceId is { } parentId
    92	                ? ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary.GetResourceByIdPattern(parentId)?.Type
    93	                : null;
    94	
    95	        /// <inheritdoc/>
    96	        ProvisioningPropertyInfo? IProvisioningPropertyInfo.GetProvisioningPropertyInfo(InputModelProperty inputProp)
    97	        {
    98	            if (!_propertyLookup.TryGetValue(inputProp, out var propInfo))
    99	                return null;
   100	            return new ProvisioningPropertyInfo(
   101	                propInfo.PropertyName,
   102	                propInfo.IsOutput,
   103	                propInfo.IsRequired,
   104	                propInfo.BicepPath,
   105	                propInfo.DefaultValue,
   106	                propInfo.TypeOverride);
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        /// <summary>
   110	        /// Constructor for base resource types (with metadata from ARM provider schema).
   111	        /// </summary>
   112	        public ProvisioningResourceProvider(InputModelType inputModel, ArmResourceMetadata metadata)
   113	            : base(inputModel)
   114	        {
   115	            _inputModel = inputModel;
   116	            _resourceMetadata = metadata;
   117	            _defaultApiVersion = metadata.ApiVersions.Count > 0
   118	                ? metadata.ApiVersions.Last()
   119	                : null;
   120	            _createBodyWritableProperties = BuildCreateBodyWritableProperties();
   121	            _allProperties = CollectAllProperties();
   122	            _propertyLookup = _allProperties.ToDictionary(p => p.Property);
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        /// <summary>
   126	        /// Constructor for derived discriminated resource types (no metadata, inherits from base resource).
   127	        /// </summary>
   128	        internal ProvisioningResourceProvider(InputModelType inputModel)
   129	            : base(inputModel)
   130	        {
   131	            _inputModel = inputModel;
   132	            _resourceMetadata = null;
   133	            _defaultApiVersion = null;
   134	            _createBodyWritableProperties = [];
   135	            _allProperties = CollectAllProperties();
   136	            _propertyLookup = _allProperties.ToDictionary(p => p.Property);
   137	        }
   138	
   139	        public override void Reset()
   140	        {
   141	            base.Reset();
   142	            _parentField = null;
   143	            _parentProperty = null;
   144	            _parentType = null;
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        protected override string BuildNamespace()
   148	            => ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.PrimaryNamespace;
   149	
   150	        protected override string BuildRelativeFilePath()
   151	            => Path.Combine("src", "Generated", $"{Name}.cs");
   152	
   153	        protected override TypeSignatureModifiers BuildDeclarationModifiers()
   154	            => TypeSignatureModifiers.Public | TypeSignatureModifiers.Partial | TypeSignatureModifiers.Class;
   155	
   156	        protected override CSharpType? BuildBaseType()
   157	        {
   158	            // Derived discriminated resources inherit from their base resource type
   159	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null && _inputModel.BaseModel != null)
   160	            {
   161	                var baseProvider = CodeModelGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateModel(_inputModel.BaseModel);
   162	                if (baseProvider != null)
   163	                    return baseProvider.Type;
   164	            }
   165	            return new CSharpType(typeof(ProvisionableResource));
   166	        }
   167	
   168	        protected override FieldProvider[] BuildFields()
   169	        {
   170	            var fields = Properties.OfType<ProvisioningPropertyProvider>().Select(p => p.BackingField!).ToList();
   171	            if (_parentField != null)
   172	            {
   173	                fields.Add(_parentField);
   174	            }
   175	            return [.. fields];
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        protected override PropertyProvider[] BuildProperties()
   179	        {
   180	            var properties = new List<PropertyProvider>();
   181	            foreach (var propInfo in _allProperties)
   182	            {
   183	                var property = CodeModelGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateProperty(propInfo.Property, this);
   184	                if (property != null)
   185	                    properties.Add(property);
   186	            }
   187	
   188	            // Create parent property for child resources
   189	            _parentType = ParentResourceType;
   190	            if (_parentType != null)
   191	            {
   192	                _parentField = new FieldProvider(
   193	                    FieldModifiers.Private,
   194	                    new CSharpType(typeof(ResourceReference<>), _parentType),
   195	                    "_parent",
   196	                    this);
   197	                _parentProperty = BuildParentProperty(_parentField, _parentType);
   198	                properties.Add(_parentProperty);
   199	            }
   200	
   201	            return [.. properties];
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        private PropertyProvider BuildParentProperty(FieldProvider parentField, CSharpType parentType)
   205	        {
   206	            var nullableParentType = parentType.WithNullable(true);
   207	
   208	            MethodBodyStatement[] parentGetter =
   209	            [
   210	                This.Invoke("Initialize").Terminate(),
   211	                Return(parentField.AsValueExpression.Property("Value"))
   212	            ];
   213	            MethodBodyStatement[] parentSetter =
   214	            [
   215	                This.Invoke("Initialize").Terminate(),
   216	                parentField.AsValueExpression.Property("Value").Assign(Value).Terminate()
   217	            ];
   218	
   219	            return new PropertyProvider(
   220	                null,
   221	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public,
   222	                nullableParentType,
   223	                "Parent",
   224	                new MethodPropertyBody(parentGetter, parentSetter),
   225	                this);
   226	        }
   227	
   228	        protected override ConstructorProvider[] BuildConstructors()
   229	        {
   230	            var bicepIdentifierParam = new ParameterProvider("bicepIdentifier", $"The bicep identifier name.", typeof(string));
   231	            var resourceVersionParam = new ParameterProvider("resourceVersion", $"The resource API version.", typeof(string), DefaultOf(new CSharpType(typeof(string), true)));
   232	
   233	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null)
   234	            {
   235	                // Derived discriminated resource: (string bicepIdentifier, string? resourceVersion = default) : base(bicepIdentifier, resourceVersion)
   236	                var initializer = new ConstructorInitializer(true, [bicepIdentifierParam, resourceVersionParam]);
   237	                var sig = new ConstructorSignature(
   238	                    Type,
   239	                    $"Creates a new {Name}.",
   240	                    MethodSignatureModifiers.Public,
   241	                    [bicepIdentifierParam, resourceVersionParam],
   242	                    null,
   243	                    initializer);
   244	                return [new ConstructorProvider(sig, MethodBodyStatement.Empty, this)];
   245	            }
   246	
   247	            // Base resource: base(bicepIdentifier, "ResourceType", resourceVersion ?? "defaultVersion")
   248	            var resourceVersionArg = _defaultApiVersion != null
   249	                ? (ValueExpression)new BinaryOperatorExpression("??",
   250	                    resourceVersionParam,
   251	                    Literal(_defaultApiVersion))
   252	                : resourceVersionParam;
   253	            var baseInitializer = new ConstructorInitializer(
   254	                true,
   255	                [
   256	                    bicepIdentifierParam,
   257	                    Literal(_resourceMetadata!.ResourceType),
   258	                    resourceVersionArg
   259	                ]);
   260	
   261	            var baseSig = new ConstructorSignature(
   262	                Type,
   263	                $"Creates a new {Name}.",
   264	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public,
   265	                [bicepIdentifierParam, resourceVersionParam],
   266	                null,
   267	                baseInitializer);
   268	
   269	            return [new ConstructorProvider(baseSig, MethodBodyStatement.Empty, this)];
   270	        }
   271	
   272	        protected override MethodProvider[] BuildMethods()
   273	        {
   274	            var methods = new List<MethodProvider>();
   275	
   276	            // DefineProvisionableProperties() override
   277	            methods.Add(BuildDefineProvisionablePropertiesMethod());
   278	
   279	            // FromExisting() static method — only for base resources
   280	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue == null)
   281	            {
   282	                methods.Add(BuildFromExistingMethod());
   283	            }
   284	
   285	            // DefineAdditionalProperties() partial method for customization
   286	            methods.Add(BuildDefineAdditionalPropertiesMethod());
   287	
   288	            // GetResourceNameRequirements() override — only for base resource types
   289	            var nameRequirementsMethod = BuildGetResourceNameRequirementsMethod(_resourceMetadata, this);
   290	            if (nameRequirementsMethod != null)
   291	            {
   292	                methods.Add(nameRequirementsMethod);
   293	            }
   294	
   295	            // CreateRoleAssignment() overloads — only for resources that have RBAC roles
   296	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue == null && _resourceMetadata?.RbacRoles?.Count > 0)
   297	            {
   298	                var outputLibrary = (ProvisioningOutputLibrary)ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
   299	                var builtInRole = outputLibrary.BuiltInRole;
   300	                if (builtInRole != null)
   301	                {
   302	                    methods.Add(BuildCreateRoleAssignmentWithIdentityMethod(builtInRole.Type));
   303	                    methods.Add(BuildCreateRoleAssignmentWithPrincipalMethod(builtInRole.Type));
   304	                }
   305	            }
   306	
   307	            return [.. methods];
   308	        }
   309	
   310	        protected override TypeProvider[] BuildNestedTypes()
   311	        {
   312	            // Derived discriminated resources don't have their own ResourceVersions
   313	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null)
   314	                return [];
   315	
   316	            var apiVersions = _resourceMetadata?.ApiVersions;
   317	            if (apiVersions == null || apiVersions.Count == 0)
   318	                return [];
   319	
   320	            // When the current (default) API version is GA, exclude preview versions.
   321	            // Preview versions are only included when the current version is itself a preview.
   322	            if (!IsPreviewApiVersion(apiVersions[^1]))
   323	            {
   324	                var gaVersions = apiVersions.Where(v => !IsPreviewApiVersion(v)).ToList();
   325	                if (gaVersions.Count == 0)
   326	                    return [];
   327	                apiVersions = gaVersions;
   328	            }
   329	
   330	            // ResourceVersions nested class
   331	            return [new ResourceVersionsProvider(this, apiVersions)];
   332	        }
   333	
   334	        protected override TypeProvider[] BuildSerializationProviders()
   335	            => [];
   336	
   337	        // ── Property collection ──────────────────────────────────────
   338	
   339	        /// <summary>
   340	        /// Builds a set of serialized property names that are writable in the create/update request body.
   341	        /// When the resource model is output-only (e.g., ProxyResource with separate create body),
   342	        /// its properties may be marked readOnly even though the create body has them as writable.
   343	        /// </summary>
   344	        private HashSet<string> BuildCreateBodyWritableProperties()
   345	        {
   346	            var result = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
   347	            if (_resourceMetadata == null) return result;
   348	
   349	            var createMethod = _resourceMetadata.Methods
   350	                .FirstOrDefault(m => m.Kind == ResourceOperationKind.Create)?.InputMethod;
   351	            if (createMethod == null) return result;
   352	
   353	            foreach (var parameter in createMethod.Parameters)
   354	            {
   355	                if (parameter.Location == InputRequestLocation.Body && parameter.Type is InputModelType bodyModel)
   356	                {
   357	                    CollectWritableProperties(bodyModel, result);
   358	                }
   359	            }
   360	
   361	            return result;
   362	        }
   363	
   364	        /// <summary>
   365	        /// Collects serialized names of writable properties from a model and its base model chain.
   366	        /// </summary>
   367	        private static void CollectWritableProperties(InputModelType model, HashSet<string> result)
   368	        {
   369	            var current = model;
   370	            while (current != null)
   371	            {
   372	                foreach (var prop in current.Properties)
   373	                {
   374	                    if (!prop.IsReadOnly)
   375	                    {
   376	                        result.Add(prop.SerializedName ?? prop.Name);
   377	                    }
   378	                }
   379	                current = current.BaseModel;
   380	            }
   381	        }
   382	
   383	        private List<ResourcePropertyInfo> CollectAllProperties()
   384	        {
   385	            // Derived discriminated resources only collect their own properties
   386	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null)
   387	                return CollectOwnProperties();
   388	
   389	            var result = new List<ResourcePropertyInfo>();
   390	            var seen = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
   391	
   392	            // Collect from the base chain first (top-most ancestor → immediate base),
   393	            // then from the resource model itself. This ensures inherited ARM common
   394	            // properties (name, location, tags) appear before leaf-defined properties
   395	            // (e.g., the "properties" bag), which controls the Bicep emission order.
   396	            var chain = new Stack<InputModelType>();
   397	            chain.Push(_inputModel);
   398	            var baseModel = _inputModel.BaseModel;
   399	            while (baseModel != null)
   400	            {
   401	                chain.Push(baseModel);
   402	                baseModel = baseModel.BaseModel;
   403	            }
   404	
   405	            foreach (var model in chain)
   406	            {
   407	                CollectPropertiesFromModel(model, result, seen, basePath: null);
   408	            }
   409	
   410	            return result;
   411	        }
   412	
   413	        private void CollectPropertiesFromModel(
   414	            InputModelType model,
   415	            List<ResourcePropertyInfo> result,
   416	            HashSet<string> seen,
   417	            string[]? basePath)
   418	        {
   419	            foreach (var prop in model.Properties)
   420	            {
   421	                if (prop.IsDiscriminator) continue;
   422	
   423	                var serializedName = prop.SerializedName ?? prop.Name;
   424	
   425	                if (seen.Contains(serializedName)) continue;
   426	                seen.Add(serializedName);
   427	
   428	                // Skip "type" property
   429	                if (SkipProperties.Contains(serializedName)) continue;
   430	
   431	                var bicepPath = basePath != null
   432	                    ? [.. basePath, serializedName]
   433	                    : new[] { serializedName };
   434	
   435	                var isOutput = (prop.IsReadOnly && !RequiredInputProperties.Contains(serializedName)
   436	                        && !_createBodyWritableProperties.Contains(serializedName))
   437	                    || OutputOnlyProperties.Contains(serializedName);
   438	                var isRequired = prop.IsRequired || RequiredInputProperties.Contains(serializedName);
   439	
   440	                var propertyName = prop.Name.ToIdentifierName();
   441	                // For singleton resources, the "name" property is output-only with a default value
   442	                string? defaultValue = null;
   443	                if (serializedName == "name"
   444	                    && _resourceMetadata?.SingletonResourceName is not null)
   445	                {
   446	                    defaultValue = _resourceMetadata.SingletonResourceName;
   447	                    isOutput = true;
   448	                }
   449	                // Ensure "location" at the resource level always uses AzureLocation,
   450	                // even when the TypeSpec defines it as plain string.
   451	                // TODO - this is currently a workaround until we have a more reliable way to detect such violations from the spec level.
   452	                CSharpType? typeOverride = null;
   453	                if (basePath is null
   454	                    && string.Equals(serializedName, "location", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
   455	                {
   456	                    typeOverride = new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), typeof(Azure.Core.AzureLocation));
   457	                }
   458	
   459	                result.Add(new ResourcePropertyInfo(prop, propertyName, bicepPath, isOutput, isRequired, defaultValue, typeOverride));
   460	            }
   461	        }
   462	
   463	        // ── Method builders ──────────────────────────────────────────
   464	
   465	        private MethodProvider BuildDefineProvisionablePropertiesMethod()
   466	        {
   467	            var statements = new List<MethodBodyStatement>();
   468	            statements.Add(Base.Invoke("DefineProvisionableProperties").Terminate());
   469	
   470	            // Emit discriminator property for derived discriminated resource types
   471	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null)
   472	            {
   473	                var discriminatorProp = FindDiscriminatorProperty();
   474	                if (discriminatorProp != null)
   475	                {
   476	                    var serializedName = discriminatorProp.SerializedName ?? discriminatorProp.Name;
   477	                    statements.Add(
   478	                        This.Invoke(
   479	                            "DefineProperty",
   480	                            [
   481	                                Literal(serializedName),
   482	                                New.Array(typeof(string), [Literal(serializedName)]),
   483	                                new PositionalParameterReferenceExpression("defaultValue", Literal(_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue))
   484	                            ],
   485	                            [typeof(string)],
   486	                            false
   487	                        ).Terminate()
   488	                    );
   489	                }
   490	            }
   491	
   492	            foreach (var provProp in Properties.OfType<ProvisioningPropertyProvider>())
   493	            {
   494	                var field = provProp.BackingField!;
   495	                string methodName;
   496	                CSharpType[] typeArgs;
   497	
   498	                if (BicepTypeHelpers.IsModelType(field.Type))
   499	                {
   500	                    methodName = "DefineModelProperty";
   501	                    typeArgs = [field.Type];
   502	                }
   503	                else if (BicepTypeHelpers.IsBicepListType(field.Type))
   504	                {
   505	                    methodName = "DefineListProperty";
   506	                    typeArgs = [BicepTypeHelpers.GetGenericArgument(field.Type)];
   507	                }
   508	                else if (BicepTypeHelpers.IsBicepDictionaryType(field.Type))
   509	                {
   510	                    methodName = "DefineDictionaryProperty";
   511	                    typeArgs = [BicepTypeHelpers.GetGenericArgument(field.Type)];
   512	                }
   513	                else
   514	                {
   515	                    methodName = "DefineProperty";
   516	                    typeArgs = [BicepTypeHelpers.GetGenericArgument(field.Type)];
   517	                }
   518	
   519	                statements.Add(field.Assign(
   520	                    This.Invoke(
   521	                        methodName,
   522	                        BicepTypeHelpers.BuildDefinePropertyArgs(provProp.Name, provProp.BicepPath, provProp.IsOutput, provProp.IsRequired, provProp.DefaultValue),
   523	                        typeArgs,
   524	                        false)
   525	                ).Terminate());
   526	            }
   527	
   528	            // Add DefineResource call for parent on child resources
   529	            if (_parentField != null && _parentType != null)
   530	            {
   531	                statements.Add(_parentField.Assign(
   532	                    This.Invoke(
   533	                        "DefineResource",
   534	                        [
   535	                            Literal("Parent"),
   536	                            New.Array(typeof(string), [Literal("parent")]),
   537	                            new PositionalParameterReferenceExpression("isRequired", Literal(true))
   538	                        ],
   539	                        [_parentType],
   540	                        false)
   541	                ).Terminate());
   542	            }
   543	
   544	            // Call the partial method for customization
   545	            statements.Add(This.Invoke("DefineAdditionalProperties").Terminate());
   546	
   547	            return new MethodProvider(
   548	                new MethodSignature(
   549	                    "DefineProvisionableProperties",
   550	                    $"Define all the provisionable properties for {Name}.",
   551	                    MethodSignatureModifiers.Protected | MethodSignatureModifiers.Override,
   552	                    null,
   553	                    null,
   554	                    []),
   555	                statements,
   556	                this);
   557	        }
   558	
   559	        private MethodProvider BuildFromExistingMethod()
   560	        {
   561	            var bicepIdentifierParam = new ParameterProvider("bicepIdentifier", $"The bicep identifier name.", typeof(string));
   562	            var resourceVersionParam = new ParameterProvider("resourceVersion", $"The resource API version.", typeof(string), DefaultOf(new CSharpType(typeof(string), true)));
   563	
   564	            var sig = new MethodSignature(
   565	                "FromExisting",
   566	                $"Creates a reference to an existing {Name}.",
   567	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public | MethodSignatureModifiers.Static,
   568	                Type,
   569	                null,
   570	                [bicepIdentifierParam, resourceVersionParam]);
   571	
   572	            // Build the body: var result = new Type(bicepIdentifier, resourceVersion); result.IsExistingResource = true; return result;
   573	            var resultVar = new VariableExpression(Type, "result");
   574	            MethodBodyStatement[] bodyStatements =
   575	            [
   576	                Declare(resultVar, New.Instance(Type, [bicepIdentifierParam, resourceVersionParam])),
   577	                resultVar.Property("IsExistingResource").Assign(True).Terminate(),
   578	                Return(resultVar)
   579	            ];
   580	
   581	            return new MethodProvider(sig, bodyStatements, this);
   582	        }
   583	
   584	        private MethodProvider BuildDefineAdditionalPropertiesMethod()
   585	        {
   586	            var sig = new MethodSignature(
   587	                "DefineAdditionalProperties",
   588	                $"Define additional provisionable properties for {Name} that are not part of the generated code.",
   589	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Partial,
   590	                null,
   591	                null,
   592	                []);
   593	
   594	            return new MethodProvider(sig, this);
   595	        }
   596	
   597	        private static MethodProvider? BuildGetResourceNameRequirementsMethod(ArmResourceMetadata? resourceMetadata, TypeProvider enclosingType)
   598	        {
   599	            if (resourceMetadata is null)
   600	            {
   601	                return null;
   602	            }
   603	
   604	            var constraints = resourceMetadata.NameConstraints;
   605	
   606	            // Only generate the override when the spec actually specifies name constraints
   607	            if (constraints.Pattern is null && constraints.MinLength is null && constraints.MaxLength is null)
   608	            {
   609	                return null;
   610	            }
   611	
   612	            int minLength = constraints.MinLength ?? 1;
   613	            int maxLength = constraints.MaxLength ?? 24;
   614	
   615	            // Parse valid characters from pattern, or use conservative default
   616	            var validCharacters = constraints.Pattern != null
   617	                ? constraints.Pattern.ParsePatternToResourceNameCharacters()
   618	                : ResourceNameCharacters.LowercaseLetters;
   619	
   620	            // If parsing produced no characters, fall back to conservative default
   621	            if (validCharacters == (ResourceNameCharacters)0)
   622	            {
   623	                validCharacters = ResourceNameCharacters.LowercaseLetters;
   624	            }
   625	
   626	            // Build the flags expression by OR-ing the individual flag values
   627	            ValueExpression flagsExpression = BuildResourceNameCharactersExpression(validCharacters);
   628	
   629	            var sig = new MethodSignature(
   630	                "GetResourceNameRequirements",
   631	                $"Get the requirements for naming this resource.",
   632	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public | MethodSignatureModifiers.Override,
   633	                typeof(ResourceNameRequirements),
   634	                $"Naming requirements.",
   635	                [],
   636	                Attributes: [new AttributeStatement(typeof(EditorBrowsableAttribute), [new MemberExpression(typeof(EditorBrowsableState), nameof(EditorBrowsableState.Never))])]);
   637	
   638	            var body = New.Instance(
   639	                typeof(ResourceNameRequirements),
   640	                [Literal(minLength), Literal(maxLength), flagsExpression]);
   641	
   642	            return new MethodProvider(sig, body, enclosingType);
   643	        }
   644	
   645	        private static ValueExpression BuildResourceNameCharactersExpression(ResourceNameCharacters characters)
   646	        {
   647	            var flags = new List<ValueExpression>();
   648	
   649	            if (characters.HasFlag(ResourceNameCharacters.LowercaseLetters))
   650	                flags.Add(FrameworkEnumValue(ResourceNameCharacters.LowercaseLetters));
   651	            if (characters.HasFlag(ResourceNameCharacters.UppercaseLetters))
   652	                flags.Add(FrameworkEnumValue(ResourceNameCharacters.UppercaseLetters));
   653	            if (characters.HasFlag(ResourceNameCharacters.Numbers))
   654	                flags.Add(FrameworkEnumValue(ResourceNameCharacters.Numbers));
   655	            if (characters.HasFlag(ResourceNameCharacters.Hyphen))
   656	                flags.Add(FrameworkEnumValue(ResourceNameCharacters.Hyphen));
   657	            if (characters.HasFlag(ResourceNameCharacters.Underscore))
   658	                flags.Add(FrameworkEnumValue(ResourceNameCharacters.Underscore));
   659	            if (characters.HasFlag(ResourceNameCharacters.Period))
   660	                flags.Add(FrameworkEnumValue(ResourceNameCharacters.Period));
   661	            if (characters.HasFlag(ResourceNameCharacters.Parentheses))
   662	                flags.Add(FrameworkEnumValue(ResourceNameCharacters.Parentheses));
   663	
   664	            // OR them together
   665	            var result = flags[0];
   666	            for (int i = 1; i < flags.Count; i++)
   667	            {
   668	                result = new BinaryOperatorExpression("|", result, flags[i]);
   669	            }
   670	            return result;
   671	        }
   672	
   673	        // ── CreateRoleAssignment helpers ─────────────────────────────
   674	
   675	        /// <summary>
   676	        /// Builds: CreateRoleAssignment(XxxBuiltInRole role, UserAssignedIdentity identity)
   677	        /// </summary>
   678	        private MethodProvider BuildCreateRoleAssignmentWithIdentityMethod(CSharpType builtInRoleType)
   679	        {
   680	            var roleParam = new ParameterProvider("role", $"The role to grant.", builtInRoleType);
   681	            var identityParam = new ParameterProvider("identity", $"The <see cref=\"UserAssignedIdentity\"/>.", typeof(UserAssignedIdentity));
   682	
   683	            var sig = new MethodSignature(
   684	                "CreateRoleAssignment",
   685	                $"Creates a role assignment for a user-assigned identity that grants access to this {Name}.",
   686	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public,
   687	                typeof(RoleAssignment),
   688	                $"The <see cref=\"RoleAssignment\"/>.",
   689	                [roleParam, identityParam]);
   690	
   691	            var resultVar = new VariableExpression(typeof(RoleAssignment), "result");
   692	            var roleNameVar = new VariableExpression(typeof(string), "roleName");
   693	
   694	            // string roleName = XxxBuiltInRole.GetBuiltInRoleName(role);
   695	            var getRoleName = Static(builtInRoleType).Invoke("GetBuiltInRoleName", [(ValueExpression)roleParam]);
   696	
   697	            // Constructor arg: $"{BicepIdentifier}_{identity.BicepIdentifier}_{roleName}"
   698	            var constructorArg = new FormattableStringExpression(
   699	                "{0}_{1}_{2}",
   700	                [
   701	                    new MemberExpression(null, "BicepIdentifier"),
   702	                    new MemberExpression(identityParam, "BicepIdentifier"),
   703	                    roleNameVar
   704	                ]);
   705	
   706	            // BicepFunction.GetSubscriptionResourceId("Microsoft.Authorization/roleDefinitions", role.ToString())
   707	            var roleDefId = Static(typeof(BicepFunction)).Invoke(
   708	                "GetSubscriptionResourceId",
   709	                [Literal("Microsoft.Authorization/roleDefinitions"), ((ValueExpression)roleParam).InvokeToString()]);
   710	
   711	            MethodBodyStatement[] body = [
   712	                Declare(roleNameVar, getRoleName),
   713	                Declare(resultVar, New.Instance(typeof(RoleAssignment), [constructorArg])),
   714	                resultVar.Property("Name").Assign(
   715	                    Static(typeof(BicepFunction)).Invoke("CreateGuid", [
   716	                        new MemberExpression(null, "Id"),
   717	                        new MemberExpression(identityParam, "PrincipalId"),
   718	                        roleDefId
   719	                    ])
   720	                ).Terminate(),
   721	                resultVar.Property("Scope").Assign(
   722	                    New.Instance(typeof(BicepIdentifierExpression), [new MemberExpression(null, "BicepIdentifier")])
   723	                ).Terminate(),
   724	                resultVar.Property("PrincipalType").Assign(
   725	                    new MemberExpression(Static(typeof(RoleManagementPrincipalType)), nameof(RoleManagementPrincipalType.ServicePrincipal))
   726	                ).Terminate(),
   727	                resultVar.Property("RoleDefinitionId").Assign(roleDefId).Terminate(),
   728	                resultVar.Property("PrincipalId").Assign(
   729	                    new MemberExpression(identityParam, "PrincipalId")
   730	                ).Terminate(),
   731	                Return(resultVar)
   732	            ];
   733	
   734	            return new MethodProvider(sig, body, this);
   735	        }
   736	
   737	        /// <summary>
   738	        /// Builds: CreateRoleAssignment(XxxBuiltInRole role, BicepValue&lt;RoleManagementPrincipalType&gt; principalType, BicepValue&lt;Guid&gt; principalId, string? bicepIdentifierSuffix)
   739	        /// </summary>
   740	        private MethodProvider BuildCreateRoleAssignmentWithPrincipalMethod(CSharpType builtInRoleType)
   741	        {
   742	            var roleParam = new ParameterProvider("role", $"The role to grant.", builtInRoleType);
   743	            var principalTypeParam = new ParameterProvider(
   744	                "principalType",
   745	                $"The type of the principal to assign to.",
   746	                new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>)).MakeGenericType([typeof(RoleManagementPrincipalType)]));
   747	            var principalIdParam = new ParameterProvider(
   748	                "principalId",
   749	                $"The principal to assign to.",
   750	                new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>)).MakeGenericType([typeof(Guid)]));
   751	            var suffixParam = new ParameterProvider(
   752	                "bicepIdentifierSuffix",
   753	                $"Optional role assignment identifier name suffix.",
   754	                new CSharpType(typeof(string), true),
   755	                DefaultOf(new CSharpType(typeof(string), true)));
   756	
   757	            var sig = new MethodSignature(
   758	                "CreateRoleAssignment",
   759	                $"Creates a role assignment for a principal that grants access to this {Name}.",
   760	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public,
   761	                typeof(RoleAssignment),
   762	                $"The <see cref=\"RoleAssignment\"/>.",
   763	                [roleParam, principalTypeParam, principalIdParam, suffixParam]);
   764	
   765	            var resultVar = new VariableExpression(typeof(RoleAssignment), "result");
   766	            var roleNameVar = new VariableExpression(typeof(string), "roleName");
   767	            var suffixSepVar = new VariableExpression(typeof(string), "suffixSep");
   768	
   769	            // string roleName = XxxBuiltInRole.GetBuiltInRoleName(role);
   770	            var getRoleName = Static(builtInRoleType).Invoke("GetBuiltInRoleName", [(ValueExpression)roleParam]);
   771	
   772	            // string suffixSep = bicepIdentifierSuffix is null ? "" : "_";
   773	            var declareSuffixSep = Declare(suffixSepVar, new TernaryConditionalExpression(
   774	                ((ValueExpression)suffixParam).Is(Null),
   775	                Literal(""),
   776	                Literal("_")));
   777	
   778	            // Constructor arg: $"{BicepIdentifier}_{roleName}{suffixSep}{bicepIdentifierSuffix}"
   779	            var constructorArg = new FormattableStringExpression(
   780	                "{0}_{1}{2}{3}",
   781	                [
   782	                    new MemberExpression(null, "BicepIdentifier"),
   783	                    roleNameVar,
   784	                    suffixSepVar,
   785	                    (ValueExpression)suffixParam
   786	                ]);
   787	
   788	            // BicepFunction.GetSubscriptionResourceId("Microsoft.Authorization/roleDefinitions", role.ToString())
   789	            var roleDefId = Static(typeof(BicepFunction)).Invoke(
   790	                "GetSubscriptionResourceId",
   791	                [Literal("Microsoft.Authorization/roleDefinitions"), ((ValueExpression)roleParam).InvokeToString()]);
   792	
   793	            MethodBodyStatement[] body = [
   794	                Declare(roleNameVar, getRoleName),
   795	                declareSuffixSep,
   796	                Declare(resultVar, New.Instance(typeof(RoleAssignment), [constructorArg])),
   797	                resultVar.Property("Name").Assign(
   798	                    Static(typeof(BicepFunction)).Invoke("CreateGuid", [
   799	                        new MemberExpression(null, "Id"),
   800	                        (ValueExpression)principalIdParam,
   801	                        roleDefId
   802	                    ])
   803	                ).Terminate(),
   804	                resultVar.Property("Scope").Assign(
   805	                    New.Instance(typeof(BicepIdentifierExpression), [new MemberExpression(null, "BicepIdentifier")])
   806	                ).Terminate(),
   807	                resultVar.Property("PrincipalType").Assign((ValueExpression)principalTypeParam).Terminate(),
   808	                resultVar.Property("RoleDefinitionId").Assign(roleDefId).Terminate(),
   809	                resultVar.Property("PrincipalId").Assign((ValueExpression)principalIdParam).Terminate(),
   810	                Return(resultVar)
   811	            ];
   812	
   813	            return new MethodProvider(sig, body, this);
   814	        }
   815	
   816	        // ── Type resolution helpers ──────────────────────────────────
   817	
   818	        private CSharpType GetPropertyType(InputModelProperty prop)
   819	        {
   820	            // TODO: Improve error message with more context about what went wrong
   821	            return CodeModelGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateCSharpType(prop.Type)
   822	                ?? throw new InvalidOperationException(
   823	                    $"Failed to resolve CSharpType for property '{prop.Name}' of type '{prop.Type}' in model '{_inputModel.Name}'.");
   824	        }
   825	
   826	        // ── Discriminator helpers ────────────────────────────────────
   827	
   828	        /// <summary>
   829	        /// Collects only the derived type's own properties (no base chain, no flattening).
   830	        /// Used for derived discriminated resources.
   831	        /// </summary>
   832	        private List<ResourcePropertyInfo> CollectOwnProperties()
   833	        {
   834	            var result = new List<ResourcePropertyInfo>();
   835	            foreach (var prop in _inputModel.Properties)
   836	            {
   837	                if (prop.IsDiscriminator) continue;
   838	                var serializedName = prop.SerializedName ?? prop.Name;
   839	                string[] bicepPath = [serializedName];
   840	                result.Add(new ResourcePropertyInfo(
   841	                    prop,
   842	                    prop.Name.ToIdentifierName(),
   843	                    bicepPath,
   844	                    prop.IsReadOnly,
   845	                    prop.IsRequired));
   846	            }
   847	            return result;
   848	        }
   849	
   850	        /// <summary>
   851	        /// Finds the discriminator property by walking up the model's base chain.
   852	        /// </summary>
   853	        private InputModelProperty? FindDiscriminatorProperty()
   854	        {
   855	            var model = _inputModel;
   856	            while (model != null)
   857	            {
   858	                if (model.DiscriminatorProperty != null)
   859	                    return model.DiscriminatorProperty;
   860	                model = model.BaseModel;
   861	            }
   862	            return null;
   863	        }
   864	
   865	        // ── Property info record ─────────────────────────────────────
   866	
   867	        internal record ResourcePropertyInfo(
   868	            InputModelProperty Property,
   869	            string PropertyName,
   870	            string[] BicepPath,
   871	            bool IsOutput,
   872	            bool IsRequired,
   873	            string? DefaultValue = null,
   874	            CSharpType? TypeOverride = null);
   875	
   876	        // ── ResourceVersions nested class ────────────────────────────
   877	
   878	        private class ResourceVersionsProvider : TypeProvider
   879	        {
   880	            private readonly ProvisioningResourceProvider _parent;
   881	            private readonly IReadOnlyList<string> _apiVersions;
   882	
   883	            public ResourceVersionsProvider(ProvisioningResourceProvider parent, IReadOnlyList<string> apiVersions)
   884	            {
   885	                _parent = parent;
   886	                _apiVersions = apiVersions;
   887	            }
   888	
   889	            protected override string BuildName() => "ResourceVersions";
   890	
   891	            protected override string BuildNamespace()
   892	                => ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.PrimaryNamespace;
   893	
   894	            protected override string BuildRelativeFilePath()
   895	                => _parent.RelativeFilePath; // Same file as parent
   896	
   897	            protected override TypeSignatureModifiers BuildDeclarationModifiers()
   898	                => TypeSignatureModifiers.Public | TypeSignatureModifiers.Static | TypeSignatureModifiers.Class;
   899	
   900	            protected override FieldProvider[] BuildFields()
   901	            {
   902	                var fields = new List<FieldProvider>();
   903	
   904	                foreach (var version in _apiVersions.Reverse())
   905	                {
   906	                    var fieldName = "V" + version.Replace('.', '_').Replace('-', '_').ToUpperInvariant();
   907	
   908	                    // Preview API versions are marked with [Experimental] to signal they may change or be removed.
   909	                    var isPreview = IsPreviewApiVersion(version);
   910	                    var attributes = isPreview
   911	                        ? [new AttributeStatement(typeof(ExperimentalAttribute), [Literal("AZPROVISION001")])]
   912	                        : Array.Empty<AttributeStatement>();
   913	
   914	                    fields.Add(new FieldProvider(
   915	                        FieldModifiers.Public | FieldModifiers.Static | FieldModifiers.ReadOnly,
   916	                        typeof(string),
   917	                        fieldName,
   918	                        this,
   919	                        description: $"API version \"{version}\".",
   920	                        initializationValue: Literal(version),
   921	                        attributes: attributes));
   922	                }
   923	
   924	                return [.. fields];
   925	            }
   926	        }
   927	
   928	        internal static bool IsPreviewApiVersion(string version)
   929	            => version.Contains("preview", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
   930	    }
   931	}

```csharp
if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(model, out var resources))
{
    if (resources.Count == 1)
    {
        return resources[0];
    }
    // Multiple resources share the same model — not yet supported
    throw new NotSupportedException(
        $"Model '{model.Name}' is shared by {resources.Count} resource types " +
        $"({string.Join(", ", resources.Select(r => r.Name))}). " +
        $"Multiple resources sharing the same model is not yet supported. " +
        $"See https://github.com/Azure/azure-sdk-for-net/issues/56733");
}
```

The PR description says:
1. Some management RPs have multiple ARM resources sharing the same resource model → we must generate multiple classes when this happens.
2. Other models might reference a resource model as a property type. If the model is shared across multiple resources, it's unclear which resource class to use as the property type.

     1	// Copyright (c) Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.
     2	// Licensed under the MIT License.
     3	
     4	using Azure.Provisioning.Resources;
     5	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Primitives;
     6	using System.Collections.Generic;
     7	using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;
     8	
     9	namespace Azure.Generator.Provisioning.Primitives
    10	{
    11	    /// <summary>
    12	    /// Known ARM common types that the provisioning generator should skip generating
    13	    /// (they have framework equivalents in Azure.Provisioning).
    14	    /// </summary>
    15	    internal static class KnownProvisioningTypes
    16	    {
    17	        /// <summary>
    18	        /// ARM inheritable base types (TrackedResource, ProxyResource, etc.).
    19	        /// Provisioning types use ProvisionableConstruct/ProvisionableResource as base instead.
    20	        /// </summary>
    21	        private static readonly HashSet<string> _inheritableSystemTypes =
    22	        [
    23	            "Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.ProxyResource",
    24	            "Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.ExtensionResource",
    25	            "Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.Resource",
    26	            "Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.TrackedResource",
    27	        ];
    28	
    29	        /// <summary>
    30	        /// Maps known ARM common type cross-language definition IDs to their Azure.Provisioning equivalents.
    31	        /// Types in this map should not be generated — the provisioning framework types are used instead.
    32	        /// </summary>
    33	        private static readonly IReadOnlyDictionary<string, CSharpType> _provisioningTypeMap = new Dictionary<string, CSharpType>()
    34	        {
    35	            // Models
    36	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.ManagedServiceIdentity"] = typeof(ManagedServiceIdentity),
    37	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.Legacy.ManagedServiceIdentityV4"] = typeof(ManagedServiceIdentity),
    38	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.SystemData"] = typeof(SystemData),
    39	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.UserAssignedIdentity"] = typeof(UserAssignedIdentityDetails),
    40	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.Plan"] = typeof(ArmPlan),
    41	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.Models.SubResource"] = typeof(SubResource),
    42	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.Models.WritableSubResource"] = typeof(WritableSubResource),
    43	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.ExtendedLocation"] = typeof(ExtendedAzureLocation),
    44	            // Enums
    45	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.ExtendedLocationType"] = typeof(ExtendedLocationType),
    46	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.ManagedServiceIdentityType"] = typeof(ManagedServiceIdentityType),
    47	            ["Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.createdByType"] = typeof(CreatedByType),
    48	        };
    49	
    50	        /// <summary>
    51	        /// Returns true if the given cross-language definition ID is a known ARM inheritable base type.
    52	        /// </summary>
    53	        public static bool IsInheritableSystemType(string crossLanguageDefinitionId)
    54	            => _inheritableSystemTypes.Contains(crossLanguageDefinitionId);
    55	
    56	        /// <summary>
    57	        /// Returns true if the given cross-language definition ID is a known ARM type
    58	        /// that has a provisioning framework equivalent and should not be generated.
    59	        /// </summary>
    60	        public static bool IsKnownType(string crossLanguageDefinitionId)
    61	            => _provisioningTypeMap.ContainsKey(crossLanguageDefinitionId);
    62	
    63	        /// <summary>
    64	        /// Tries to get the Azure.Provisioning equivalent type for a known ARM common type.
    65	        /// </summary>
    66	        public static bool TryGetProvisioningType(string crossLanguageDefinitionId, [MaybeNullWhen(false)] out CSharpType type)
    67	            => _provisioningTypeMap.TryGetValue(crossLanguageDefinitionId, out type);
    68	    }
    69	}

    11	/// <summary> Represents the metadata for an ARM resource, including its identity, scope, methods, and hierarchy. </summary>
    12	/// <param name="ResourceIdPattern"> The ARM resource ID pattern. </param>
    13	/// <param name="ResourceName"> The resource name. </param>
    14	/// <param name="ResourceType"> The ARM resource type. </param>
    15	/// <param name="ResourceModel"> The input model type for the resource. </param>
    16	/// <param name="Scope"> The scope information for the resource. </param>
    17	/// <param name="Methods"> The list of methods associated with the resource. </param>
    18	/// <param name="SingletonResourceName"> The singleton resource name, if applicable. </param>
    19	/// <param name="ParentResourceId"> The parent resource ID pattern, if applicable. </param>
    20	/// <param name="ChildResourceIds"> The list of child resource ID patterns. </param>
    21	/// <param name="NameConstraints"> The name constraints for the resource. </param>
    22	/// <param name="ApiVersions"> The API versions that this resource is available in. </param>
    23	/// <param name="RbacRoles"> The RBAC roles defined for this resource. </param>
    24	public record ArmResourceMetadata(
    25	    RequestPathPattern ResourceIdPattern,
    26	    string ResourceName,
    27	    string ResourceType,
    28	    InputModelType ResourceModel,
    29	    ArmScopeInfo Scope,
    30	    IReadOnlyList<ResourceMethod> Methods,
    31	    string? SingletonResourceName,
    32	    RequestPathPattern? ParentResourceId,
    33	    IReadOnlyList<RequestPathPattern> ChildResourceIds,
    34	    ArmResourceNameConstraints NameConstraints,
    35	    IReadOnlyList<string> ApiVersions,
    36	    IReadOnlyList<ArmResourceRbacRole> RbacRoles)
    37	{
    38	    // ChildResourceIds is currently unpopulated and passed in as an empty array
    39	    internal static ArmResourceMetadata DeserializeResourceMetadata(JsonElement element, InputModelType inputModel, IReadOnlyList<RequestPathPattern> childResourceIds)
    40	    {
    41	        string? resourceIdPattern = null;
    42	        string? resourceType = null;
    43	        string? singletonResourceName = null;
    44	        ArmScopeInfo? scope = null;
    45	        var methods = new List<ResourceMethod>();
    46	        string? parentResource = null;
    47	        string? resourceName = null;
    48	
    49	        if (element.TryGetProperty("resourceIdPattern", out var resourceIdPatternElement))
    50	        {
    51	            resourceIdPattern = resourceIdPatternElement.GetString();
    52	        }
    53	        if (element.TryGetProperty("resourceType", out var resourceTypeElement))
    54	        {
    55	            resourceType = resourceTypeElement.GetString();
    56	        }
    57	        if (element.TryGetProperty("singletonResourceName", out var singletonResourceElement))
    58	        {
    59	            singletonResourceName = singletonResourceElement.GetString();
    60	        }
    61	        if (element.TryGetProperty("scope", out var scopeElement))
    62	        {
    63	            scope = ArmScopeInfo.Deserialize(scopeElement);
    64	        }
    65	        if (element.TryGetProperty("methods", out var methodsElement))
    66	        {
    67	            foreach (var item in methodsElement.EnumerateArray())
    68	            {
    69	                methods.Add(ResourceMethod.DeserializeResourceMethod(item));
    70	            }
    71	        }
    72	        if (element.TryGetProperty("parentResourceId", out var parentResourceElement))
    73	        {
    74	            parentResource = parentResourceElement.GetString();
    75	        }
    76	        if (element.TryGetProperty("resourceName", out var resourceNameElement))
    77	        {
    78	            resourceName = resourceNameElement.GetString();
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        ArmResourceNameConstraints nameConstraints = new(null, null, null);
    82	        if (element.TryGetProperty("nameConstraints", out var nameConstraintsElement))
    83	        {
    84	            nameConstraints = ArmResourceNameConstraints.DeserializeNameConstraints(nameConstraintsElement);
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        var apiVersions = new List<string>();
    88	        if (element.TryGetProperty("apiVersions", out var apiVersionsElement))
    89	        {
    90	            foreach (var item in apiVersionsElement.EnumerateArray())
    91	            {
    92	                var version = item.GetString();
    93	                if (version is not null)
    94	                {
    95	                    apiVersions.Add(version);
    96	                }
    97	            }
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        var rbacRoles = new List<ArmResourceRbacRole>();
   101	        if (element.TryGetProperty("rbacRoles", out var rbacRolesElement))
   102	        {
   103	            foreach (var item in rbacRolesElement.EnumerateArray())
   104	            {
   105	                rbacRoles.Add(ArmResourceRbacRole.DeserializeRbacRole(item));
   106	            }
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        return new(
   110	            new RequestPathPattern(resourceIdPattern ?? throw new InvalidOperationException("resourceIdPattern cannot be null")),
   111	            resourceName ?? throw new InvalidOperationException("resourceName cannot be null"),
   112	            resourceType ?? throw new InvalidOperationException("resourceType cannot be null"),
   113	            inputModel,
   114	            scope ?? throw new InvalidOperationException("scope cannot be null"),
   115	            methods,
   116	            singletonResourceName,
   117	            parentResource is not null ? new RequestPathPattern(parentResource) : null,
   118	            childResourceIds,
   119	            nameConstraints,
   120	            apiVersions,
   121	            rbacRoles);
   122	    }
   123	}

     1	// Copyright (c) Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.
     2	// Licensed under the MIT License.
     3	
     4	using System;
     5	using System.Collections.Generic;
     6	using System.Text.Json;
     7	
     8	namespace Azure.Generator.Management.Models;
     9	
    10	/// <summary>
    11	/// Represents the unified ARM provider schema containing all resource metadata and non-resource methods.
    12	/// This consolidates information previously scattered across @resourceSchema and @nonResourceMethodSchema decorators.
    13	/// </summary>
    14	public class ArmProviderSchema
    15	{
    16	    /// <summary> Gets the list of ARM resource metadata. </summary>
    17	    public IReadOnlyList<ArmResourceMetadata> Resources { get; }
    18	
    19	    /// <summary> Gets the list of non-resource methods. </summary>
    20	    public IReadOnlyList<NonResourceMethod> NonResourceMethods { get; }
    21	
    22	    /// <summary> Initializes a new instance of <see cref="ArmProviderSchema"/>. </summary>
    23	    /// <param name="resources"> The list of resource metadata. </param>
    24	    /// <param name="nonResourceMethods"> The list of non-resource methods. </param>
    25	    public ArmProviderSchema(IReadOnlyList<ArmResourceMetadata> resources, IReadOnlyList<NonResourceMethod> nonResourceMethods)
    26	    {
    27	        Resources = resources;
    28	        NonResourceMethods = nonResourceMethods;
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    /// <summary>
    32	    /// Deserializes the ArmProviderSchema from decorator arguments.
    33	    /// </summary>
    34	    /// <param name="arguments">The decorator arguments containing resources and nonResourceMethods data</param>
    35	    /// <param name="library">The management input library containing models cache</param>
    36	    /// <param name="methodFilter">Optional predicate to filter non-resource methods</param>
    37	    /// <returns>A new ArmProviderSchema instance</returns>
    38	    public static ArmProviderSchema Deserialize(IReadOnlyDictionary<string, BinaryData> arguments, ManagementInputLibrary library, Func<NonResourceMethod, bool>? methodFilter = null)
    39	    {
    40	        var resourceMetadata = new List<ArmResourceMetadata>();
    41	        var resourceChildren = new Dictionary<string, List<RequestPathPattern>>();
    42	
    43	        // Deserialize resources
    44	        if (arguments.TryGetValue("resources", out var resourcesData))
    45	        {
    46	            using var document = JsonDocument.Parse(resourcesData);
    47	            foreach (var item in document.RootElement.EnumerateArray())
    48	            {
    49	                var resourceModelId = item.GetProperty("resourceModelId").GetString();
    50	                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(resourceModelId))
    51	                {
    52	                    continue;
    53	                }
    54	
    55	                if (!library.ModelsByCrossLanguageDefinitionId.TryGetValue(resourceModelId, out var model))
    56	                {
    57	                    ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.Emitter.ReportDiagnostic(
    58	                        "general-warning",
    59	                        $"Model with cross-language definition ID '{resourceModelId}' not found in namespace. This resource will be skipped.",
    60	                        targetCrossLanguageDefinitionId: resourceModelId);
    61	                    continue;
    62	                }
    63	
    64	                var children = new List<RequestPathPattern>();
    65	                var metadata = ArmResourceMetadata.DeserializeResourceMetadata(item, model, children);
    66	                resourceMetadata.Add(metadata);
    67	                resourceChildren.Add(metadata.ResourceIdPattern, children);
    68	            }
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        // Second pass to fulfill the children list
    72	        foreach (var resource in resourceMetadata)
    73	        {
    74	            if (resource.ParentResourceId is not null)
    75	            {
    76	                resourceChildren[resource.ParentResourceId].Add(resource.ResourceIdPattern);
    77	            }
    78	        }
    79	
    80	        // Deserialize non-resource methods
    81	        var nonResourceMethods = new List<NonResourceMethod>();
    82	        if (arguments.TryGetValue("nonResourceMethods", out var nonResourceMethodsData))
    83	        {
    84	            using var document = JsonDocument.Parse(nonResourceMethodsData);
    85	            foreach (var item in document.RootElement.EnumerateArray())
    86	            {
    87	                var nonResourceMethod = NonResourceMethod.DeserializeNonResourceMethod(item);
    88	
    89	                // Apply filter if provided
    90	                if (methodFilter == null || methodFilter(nonResourceMethod))
    91	                {
    92	                    nonResourceMethods.Add(nonResourceMethod);
    93	                }
    94	            }
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        return new ArmProviderSchema(resourceMetadata, nonResourceMethods);
    98	    }
    99	}

2026-06-01 03:41:29,227 - INFO - swea-agent-Azure__azure-sdk-for-net-58482 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a clear picture. Let me think about the solution:

The problem is:
1. **Multiple resource providers share the same model**: `ProvisioningOutputLibrary` creates one `ProvisioningResourceProvider` per `ArmResourceMetadata`, and maps them by model. If multiple resources share the same model, `_resourcesByModel` has a list with multiple items. In `CreateModelCore`, when this happens, it currently throws `NotSupportedException`.

2. **Property type references**: When another model references a resource model as a property type, and that model is shared across multiple resources, it's unclear which resource class to use.

The fix should:
- When multiple resources share the same model, generate one `ProvisioningResourceProvider` class per resource type (using the resource name from metadata to differentiate them), instead of trying to return a single one.
- But wait — `CreateModelCore` is called once per `InputModelType`. If multiple resources share the same model, we can't return multiple providers from `CreateModelCore`. 

Let me re-read the `ProvisioningOutputLibrary.BuildTypeProviders()`:

```csharp
protected override TypeProvider[] BuildTypeProviders()
{
    var providers = new List<TypeProvider>();

    // Add resource providers and mark them to survive post-processing.
    foreach (var resource in Resources)
    {
        providers.Add(resource);
        ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.AddTypeToKeep(resource.Name);
    }
    ...
    foreach (var inputModel in inputLib.InputNamespace.Models)
    {
        var model = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateModel(inputModel);
        if (model is not null && model is not ProvisioningResourceProvider)
        {
            providers.Add(model);
        }
    }
    ...
}
```

So resources are already added directly from `Resources` list (one per `ArmResourceMetadata`). And then when iterating models, `CreateModel` is called which goes to `CreateModelCore`. When a model is a resource model, it returns the resource provider (which is already in the list from the first loop), and it's filtered out (`model is not ProvisioningResourceProvider`).

The issue is that `CreateModelCore` assumes there's exactly one resource per model. When there are multiple, it currently throws. The fix should:
1. Return `null` (or one of the resources) when multiple resources share the model, since all resources are already added via the first loop.
2. This means the model is still "claimed" as a resource model, so it won't be turned into a `ProvisioningModelProvider`.

But wait, there's another call path. Let me check who calls `CreateModelCore` besides `BuildTypeProviders`:

1. `BuildTypeProviders` - iterates all input models, calls `CreateModel`, filters out `ProvisioningResourceProvider`
2. `ProvisioningResourceProvider.BuildBaseType()` - for derived discriminated resources, it calls `CreateModel` on the base model
3. Property type resolution - `CreateCSharpTypeCore` for model types

For case 3, when a property references a model that is a resource model, it needs to resolve to the correct resource type. If multiple resources share the model, which one should be the property type?

Let me look at the PR description again: "Additionally, other models might reference a resource model as a property type. If the model is shared across multiple resources, it's unclear which resource class to use as the property type."

The solution in the original PR (azure-sdk-for-net#56627) likely:
1. When multiple resources share the same model, still generate multiple resource classes (one per resource type). This is already done because resources are added from the `Resources` list directly.
2. In `CreateModelCore`, instead of throwing, return `null` so the model is not treated as a resource model. But then the model would be created as a `ProvisioningModelProvider`...

Wait, let me re-examine. Maybe the approach is: when there are multiple resources for a model, return `null` from `CreateModelCore`, which means the model falls through to being created as a `ProvisioningModelProvider` — a regular model. But then the resource providers still exist (they were added directly from `Resources`). Each resource provider can have its own name derived from the resource metadata, not from the model.

But the problem is: if the model is created as a `ProvisioningModelProvider`, it won't be a `ProvisionableResource`. Properties that reference this model would get the `ProvisioningModelProvider` type, not any of the resource types.

Let me think about this more carefully. Looking at the original PR:

- PR #56627 in azure-sdk-for-net - "Handle multiple resources sharing the same resource model"
- The current code throws `NotSupportedException` when multiple resources share the same model

I think the fix should be:
1. In `CreateModelCore`, instead of throwing when `resources.Count > 1`, return `null` (the model is not a resource model in the traditional sense — there are multiple resources derived from it).
2. The resources are already generated from the `Resources` loop in `BuildTypeProviders`.
3. The model itself should be generated as a `ProvisioningModelProvider` (a `ProvisionableConstruct`), since it's the shared data model.
4. Each resource provider class should then reference/use this shared model.

But wait, currently `ProvisioningResourceProvider` extends `ModelProvider`. If we generate a separate `ProvisioningModelProvider` for the same model, there would be duplicate properties.

Actually, let me look again at how the current flow works for single-resource case:
- `BuildTypeProviders` adds `ProvisioningResourceProvider` directly from `Resources`
- Then iterates models, calls `CreateModel`, which returns the same `ProvisioningResourceProvider`, and it's filtered out
- The `ProvisioningResourceProvider` generates the `ProvisionableResource` subclass

For the multi-resource case:
- `BuildTypeProviders` adds multiple `ProvisioningResourceProvider` from `Resources` (one per resource)
- Then iterates models, calls `CreateModel` for the shared model → currently throws

The fix should allow `CreateModel` to return something sensible. If it returns `null`, then the model falls through to become a `ProvisioningModelProvider`. But then we'd have both `ProvisioningResourceProvider` and `ProvisioningModelProvider` for the same model, which seems wrong.

Hmm, let me think again. Let me look at how resource data model vs resource class works:

In the provisioning pattern:
- `ProvisioningResourceProvider` generates a class like `KeyVaultService` that extends `ProvisionableResource` 
- It includes properties from its model (like `KeyVaultServiceData` properties)
- But it also includes system properties (name, location, tags, id, systemData)

When multiple resources share the same data model, they each get their own `ProvisionableResource` subclass, but they share the same data properties. For the data model itself, we probably want a `ProvisionableConstruct` subclass that both resource types can reference.

Actually, I think the correct approach is:
1. When there are multiple resources sharing the same model, `CreateModelCore` should return `null` (not throw), so the model is treated as a non-resource model.
2. But wait — that would make it a `ProvisioningModelProvider`, and there would be duplicate property definitions.

Let me look at the `ProvisioningModelProvider`:

    23	    /// <summary>
    24	    /// Generates a ProvisionableConstruct subclass from an InputModelType.
    25	    /// Uses TypeFactory.CreateCSharpType() for all type resolution, which returns
    26	    /// BicepValue&lt;T&gt; / BicepList&lt;T&gt; / BicepDictionary&lt;T&gt; types directly.
    27	    /// </summary>
    28	    internal class ProvisioningModelProvider : ModelProvider, IProvisioningPropertyInfo
    29	    {
    30	        private readonly InputModelType _inputModel;
    31	
    32	        public ProvisioningModelProvider(InputModelType inputModel) : base(inputModel)
    33	        {
    34	            _inputModel = inputModel;
    35	        }
    36	
    37	        protected override string BuildNamespace()
    38	            => ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.PrimaryNamespace;
    39	
    40	        protected override string BuildRelativeFilePath()
    41	            => Path.Combine("src", "Generated", "Models", $"{Name}.cs");
    42	
    43	        protected override TypeSignatureModifiers BuildDeclarationModifiers()
    44	            => TypeSignatureModifiers.Public | TypeSignatureModifiers.Partial | TypeSignatureModifiers.Class;
    45	
    46	        protected override CSharpType? BuildBaseType()
    47	        {
    48	            // Derived discriminated types inherit from their base model type
    49	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null && _inputModel.BaseModel != null)
    50	            {
    51	                var baseProvider = CodeModelGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateModel(_inputModel.BaseModel);
    52	                if (baseProvider != null)
    53	                    return baseProvider.Type;
    54	            }
    55	            return new CSharpType(typeof(ProvisionableConstruct));
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        /// <inheritdoc/>
    59	        ProvisioningPropertyInfo? IProvisioningPropertyInfo.GetProvisioningPropertyInfo(InputModelProperty property)
    60	        {
    61	            if (property.IsDiscriminator) return null;
    62	            var serializedName = property.SerializedName ?? property.Name;
    63	            return new ProvisioningPropertyInfo(
    64	                property.Name.ToIdentifierName(),
    65	                property.IsReadOnly,
    66	                property.IsRequired,
    67	                [serializedName]);
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        protected override FieldProvider[] BuildFields()
    71	        {
    72	            return [.. Properties.OfType<ProvisioningPropertyProvider>().Select(p => p.BackingField!)];
    73	        }
    74	
    75	        protected override PropertyProvider[] BuildProperties()
    76	        {
    77	            var properties = new List<PropertyProvider>();
    78	            var seen = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    79	
    80	            // Collect properties from the model and its base chain.
    81	            // Non-discriminated models use ProvisionableConstruct as C# base (not the TypeSpec base),
    82	            // so inherited properties must be explicitly collected here.
    83	            var model = _inputModel;
    84	            while (model != null)
    85	            {
    86	                foreach (var prop in model.Properties)
    87	                {
    88	                    if (prop.IsDiscriminator) continue;
    89	                    if (!seen.Add(prop.Name)) continue;
    90	
    91	                    var property = CodeModelGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateProperty(prop, this);
    92	                    if (property != null)
    93	                        properties.Add(property);
    94	                }
    95	                // Discriminated types use C# inheritance, so only collect own properties
    96	                if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null) break;
    97	                model = model.BaseModel;
    98	            }
    99	            return [.. properties];
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        protected override ConstructorProvider[] BuildConstructors()
   103	        {
   104	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null)
   105	            {
   106	                // Derived discriminated model: () : base()
   107	                var initializer = new ConstructorInitializer(true, Array.Empty<ValueExpression>());
   108	                var sig = new ConstructorSignature(
   109	                    Type,
   110	                    $"Creates a new {Name}.",
   111	                    MethodSignatureModifiers.Public,
   112	                    [],
   113	                    null,
   114	                    initializer);
   115	                return [new ConstructorProvider(sig, MethodBodyStatement.Empty, this)];
   116	            }
   117	
   118	            var regularSig = new ConstructorSignature(
   119	                Type,
   120	                $"Creates a new {Name}.",
   121	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public,
   122	                []);
   123	            return [new ConstructorProvider(regularSig, MethodBodyStatement.Empty, this)];
   124	        }
   125	
   126	        protected override MethodProvider[] BuildMethods()
   127	        {
   128	            var statements = new List<MethodBodyStatement>();
   129	            statements.Add(Base.Invoke("DefineProvisionableProperties").Terminate());
   130	
   131	            // Emit discriminator property for derived discriminated types
   132	            if (_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue != null)
   133	            {
   134	                var discriminatorProp = FindDiscriminatorProperty();
   135	                if (discriminatorProp != null)
   136	                {
   137	                    var serializedName = discriminatorProp.SerializedName ?? discriminatorProp.Name;
   138	                    statements.Add(
   139	                        This.Invoke(
   140	                            "DefineProperty",
   141	                            [
   142	                                Literal(serializedName),
   143	                                New.Array(typeof(string), [Literal(serializedName)]),
   144	                                new PositionalParameterReferenceExpression("defaultValue", Literal(_inputModel.DiscriminatorValue))
   145	                            ],
   146	                            [typeof(string)],
   147	                            false
   148	                        ).Terminate()
   149	                    );
   150	                }
   151	            }
   152	
   153	            foreach (var provProp in Properties.OfType<ProvisioningPropertyProvider>())
   154	            {
   155	                var field = provProp.BackingField!;
   156	                string methodName;
   157	                CSharpType[] typeArgs;
   158	
   159	                if (BicepTypeHelpers.IsModelType(field.Type))
   160	                {
   161	                    methodName = "DefineModelProperty";
   162	                    typeArgs = [field.Type];
   163	                }
   164	                else if (BicepTypeHelpers.IsBicepListType(field.Type))
   165	                {
   166	                    methodName = "DefineListProperty";
   167	                    typeArgs = [BicepTypeHelpers.GetGenericArgument(field.Type)];
   168	                }
   169	                else if (BicepTypeHelpers.IsBicepDictionaryType(field.Type))
   170	                {
   171	                    methodName = "DefineDictionaryProperty";
   172	                    typeArgs = [BicepTypeHelpers.GetGenericArgument(field.Type)];
   173	                }
   174	                else
   175	                {
   176	                    methodName = "DefineProperty";
   177	                    typeArgs = [BicepTypeHelpers.GetGenericArgument(field.Type)];
   178	                }
   179	
   180	                statements.Add(field.Assign(
   181	                    This.Invoke(
   182	                        methodName,
   183	                        BicepTypeHelpers.BuildDefinePropertyArgs(provProp.Name, provProp.BicepPath, provProp.IsOutput, provProp.IsRequired, provProp.DefaultValue),
   184	                        typeArgs,
   185	                        false)
   186	                ).Terminate());
   187	            }
   188	
   189	            var method = new MethodProvider(
   190	                new MethodSignature(
   191	                    "DefineProvisionableProperties",
   192	                    $"Define all the provisionable properties for {Name}.",
   193	                    MethodSignatureModifiers.Protected | MethodSignatureModifiers.Override,
   194	                    null,
   195	                    null,
   196	                    []),
   197	                statements,
   198	                this);
   199	
   200	            return [method];
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        protected override TypeProvider[] BuildSerializationProviders()
   204	            => [];
   205	
   206	        // ── Discriminator helpers ────────────────────────────────────
   207	
   208	        /// <summary>
   209	        /// Finds the discriminator property by walking up the model's base chain.
   210	        /// </summary>
   211	        private InputModelProperty? FindDiscriminatorProperty()
   212	        {
   213	            var model = _inputModel;
   214	            while (model != null)
   215	            {
   216	                if (model.DiscriminatorProperty != null)
   217	                    return model.DiscriminatorProperty;
   218	                model = model.BaseModel;
   219	            }
   220	            return null;
   221	        }
   222	
   223	        // ── Type resolution helpers ──────────────────────────────────
   224	
   225	        private CSharpType GetPropertyType(InputModelProperty prop)
   226	        {
   227	            return CodeModelGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateCSharpType(prop.Type)
   228	                ?? new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), typeof(object));
   229	        }
