     1	// Copyright (c) Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.
     2	// Licensed under the MIT License.
     3	
     4	using Azure.Generator.Management;
     5	using Azure.Generator.Provisioning.Primitives;
     6	using Azure.Generator.Provisioning.Providers;
     7	using Azure.Provisioning;
     8	using Azure.Provisioning.Primitives;
     9	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Input;
    10	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Input.Extensions;
    11	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Primitives;
    12	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Providers;
    13	using System;
    14	using System.Linq;
    15	
    16	namespace Azure.Generator.Provisioning
    17	{
    18	    /// <summary>
    19	    /// TypeFactory for provisioning generator that intercepts model/enum creation
    20	    /// to return provisioning-style type providers (ProvisionableConstruct/ProvisionableResource)
    21	    /// instead of management-style types.
    22	    /// </summary>
    23	    public class ProvisioningTypeFactory : ManagementTypeFactory
    24	    {
    25	        /// <summary>
    26	        /// Builds the resource provider name from the provisioning namespace.
    27	        /// For instance, "Azure.Provisioning.KeyVault" returns "KeyVault".
    28	        /// </summary>
    29	        protected override string BuildResourceProviderName()
    30	        {
    31	            const string provisioningNamespacePrefix = "Azure.Provisioning.";
    32	            if (PrimaryNamespace.StartsWith(provisioningNamespacePrefix))
    33	            {
    34	                return PrimaryNamespace[provisioningNamespacePrefix.Length..].ToIdentifierName();
    35	            }
    36	            return base.BuildResourceProviderName();
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        /// <inheritdoc/>
    40	        protected override CSharpType? CreateCSharpTypeCore(InputType inputType)
    41	        {
    42	            // For model types, check if there's a provisioning-specific type mapping first
    43	            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModel
    44	                && KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputModel.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provisioningType))
    45	            {
    46	                return provisioningType;
    47	            }
    48	
    49	            // For enum types, check provisioning mapping too (e.g., ManagedServiceIdentityType)
    50	            if (inputType is InputEnumType inputEnum
    51	                && KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputEnum.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provisioningEnumType))
    52	            {
    53	                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), provisioningEnumType);
    54	            }
    55	
    56	            // Let the mgmt base resolve known system types (ResourceIdentifier, AzureLocation, etc.)
    57	            var mgmtType = base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);
    58	
    59	            // For model types: if resolved to a system type that'\''s a ProvisionableConstruct, return as-is.
    60	            // Otherwise, for non-ProvisionableConstruct system types (ResponseError from mgmt),
    61	            // wrap in BicepValue<T> since they can'\''t be used with DefineModelProperty.
    62	            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModelType)
    63	            {
    64	                // If base resolution returned null (e.g., model shared by multiple resources),
    65	                // look up the resources directly and use the first resource'\''s type.
    66	                if (mgmtType == null)
    67	                {
    68	                    var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
    69	                    if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(inputModelType, out var sharedResources) && sharedResources.Count > 0)
    70	                    {
    71	                        mgmtType = sharedResources[0].Type;
    72	                    }
    73	                }
    74	
    75	                if (mgmtType != null && mgmtType.IsFrameworkType
    76	                    && !typeof(ProvisionableConstruct).IsAssignableFrom(mgmtType.FrameworkType))
    77	                {
    78	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
    79	                }
    80	                return mgmtType;
    81	            }
    82	            // Otherwise, for non-ProvisionableConstruct system types (ResponseError from mgmt),
    83	            // wrap in BicepValue<T> since they can't be used with DefineModelProperty.
    84	            if (inputType is InputModelType)
    85	            {
    86	                if (mgmtType != null && mgmtType.IsFrameworkType
    87	                    && !typeof(ProvisionableConstruct).IsAssignableFrom(mgmtType.FrameworkType))
    88	                {
    89	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
    90	                }
    91	                return mgmtType;
    92	            }
    93	
    94	            // For enum types, wrap in BicepValue<T>
    95	            // System enums: mgmtType is the system CSharpType
    96	            // Non-system enums: mgmtType is our ProvisioningEnumProvider.Type
    97	            if (inputType is InputEnumType)
    98	            {
    99	                if (mgmtType != null)
   100	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
   101	                // Fallback: shouldn't happen now that ProvisioningEnumProvider is wired up
   102	                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), typeof(string));
   103	            }
   104	
   105	            // For array types, produce BicepList<T> — element type should NOT be BicepValue-wrapped
   106	            if (inputType is InputArrayType arrayType)
   107	            {
   108	                var elementType = GetUnwrappedCSharpType(arrayType.ValueType);
   109	                if (elementType != null)
   110	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepList<>), elementType);
   111	            }
   112	
   113	            // For dictionary types, produce BicepDictionary<TValue> — value type should NOT be BicepValue-wrapped
   114	            if (inputType is InputDictionaryType dictType)
   115	            {
   116	                var valueType = GetUnwrappedCSharpType(dictType.ValueType);
   117	                if (valueType != null)
   118	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepDictionary<>), valueType);
   119	            }
   120	
   121	            // For all other non-model, non-enum types resolved by base (primitives, date/time, duration, etc.),
   122	            // wrap in BicepValue<T>
   123	            if (mgmtType != null)
   124	            {
   125	                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
   126	            }
   127	
   128	            return mgmtType;
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        /// <summary>
   132	        /// Resolves an InputType to its raw CSharpType without BicepValue wrapping.
   133	        /// Used for BicepList/BicepDictionary element types which handle wrapping internally.
   134	        /// </summary>
   135	        private CSharpType? GetUnwrappedCSharpType(InputType inputType)
   136	        {
   137	            // For model types, check provisioning mapping first, then fall back to base
   138	            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModel)
   139	            {
   140	                if (KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputModel.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provType))
   141	                    return provType;
   142	                return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType) ?? CreateCSharpType(inputType);
   143	            }
   144	
   145	            // For enum types, check provisioning mapping first, then fall back to base
   146	            if (inputType is InputEnumType inputEnum)
   147	            {
   148	                if (KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputEnum.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provEnumType))
   149	                    return provEnumType;
   150	                return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType) ?? typeof(string);
   151	            }
   152	
   153	            // For all other types, use the base resolution (returns raw .NET type)
   154	            return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   158	        protected override ModelProvider? CreateModelCore(InputModelType model)
   159	        {
   160	            // Known provisioning types (ManagedServiceIdentity, SystemData, etc.) → null (use framework type)
   161	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsKnownType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   162	                return null;
   163	
   164	            // Inheritable system types (TrackedResource, ProxyResource, etc.) → null
   165	            // Provisioning types use ProvisionableConstruct/ProvisionableResource as base, not ARM base types
   166	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsInheritableSystemType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   167	                return null;
   168	
   169	            // "Unknown" discriminator variants are for deserialization fallback in client SDKs.
   170	            // Provisioning types are write-only (compiled to Bicep), so we skip them.
   171	            if (model.IsUnknownDiscriminatorModel)
   172	                return null;
   173	
   174	            // Resource models → look up from output library's pre-created resource providers
   175	            var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
   176	            if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(model, out var resources))
   177	            {
   178	                if (resources.Count == 1)
   179	                {
   180	                    return resources[0];
   181	                }
   182	                // Multiple resources share the same model — all resource providers
   183	                // are already added via the Resources list in BuildTypeProviders.
   184	                // Return null here so the model itself is not treated as a resource model,
   185	                // preventing duplicate type generation. For property type resolution,
   186	                // the first resource'\''s type is used (see CreateCSharpTypeCore).
   187	                return null;
   188	                    $"({string.Join(", ", resources.Select(r => r.Name))}). " +
   189	                    $"Multiple resources sharing the same model is not yet supported. " +
   190	                    $"See https://github.com/Azure/azure-sdk-for-net/issues/56733");
   191	            }
   192	
   193	            // Derived discriminated resource types → ProvisioningResourceProvider (derived path)
   194	            if (model.DiscriminatorValue != null && IsBaseChainResource(model))
   195	            {
   196	                return new ProvisioningResourceProvider(model);
   197	            }
   198	
   199	            // Regular models (including discriminated models) → ProvisioningModelProvider
   200	            return new ProvisioningModelProvider(model);
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        /// <summary>
   204	        /// Checks whether any model in the base chain is a resource model.
   205	        /// </summary>
   206	        private bool IsBaseChainResource(InputModelType model)
   207	        {
   208	            var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
   209	            var baseModel = model.BaseModel;
   210	            while (baseModel != null)
   211	            {
   212	                if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(baseModel, out _))
   213	                    return true;
   214	                baseModel = baseModel.BaseModel;
   215	            }
   216	            return false;
   217	        }
   218	
   219	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   220	        protected override EnumProvider? CreateEnumCore(InputEnumType enumType, TypeProvider? declaringType)
   221	        {
   222	            // Known provisioning enums → null (use framework type)
   223	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsKnownType(enumType.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   224	                return null;
   225	
   226	            // Regular enums → ProvisioningEnumProvider
   227	            return new ProvisioningEnumProvider(enumType);
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   231	        protected override PropertyProvider? CreatePropertyCore(InputProperty inputProperty, TypeProvider enclosingType)
   232	        {
   233	            // Run base chain which creates property and applies visitor renames (e.g., etag → ETag).
   234	            var baseProperty = base.CreatePropertyCore(inputProperty, enclosingType);
   235	
   236	            if (inputProperty is not InputModelProperty inputModelProperty)
   237	                return baseProperty;
   238	
   239	            if (enclosingType is IProvisioningPropertyInfo infoProvider)
   240	            {
   241	                var info = infoProvider.GetProvisioningPropertyInfo(inputModelProperty);
   242	                if (info == null) return null;
   243	                var resolvedName = baseProperty?.Name ?? info.PropertyName;
   244	                var bicepType = info.TypeOverride ?? CreateCSharpType(inputModelProperty.Type);
   245	                if (bicepType == null) return null;
   246	
   247	                return ProvisioningPropertyProvider.Create(
   248	                    resolvedName, bicepType,
   249	                    info.IsOutput, info.IsRequired, info.BicepPath, info.DefaultValue,
   250	                    enclosingType);
   251	            }
   252	
   253	            return baseProperty;
   254	        }
   255	    }
   256	}

// Copyright (c) Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.
// Licensed under the MIT License.

using Azure.Generator.Management;
using Azure.Generator.Provisioning.Primitives;
using Azure.Generator.Provisioning.Providers;
using Azure.Provisioning;
using Azure.Provisioning.Primitives;
using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Input;
using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Input.Extensions;
using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Primitives;
using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Providers;
using System;
using System.Linq;

namespace Azure.Generator.Provisioning
{
    /// <summary>
    /// TypeFactory for provisioning generator that intercepts model/enum creation
    /// to return provisioning-style type providers (ProvisionableConstruct/ProvisionableResource)
    /// instead of management-style types.
    /// </summary>
    public class ProvisioningTypeFactory : ManagementTypeFactory
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Builds the resource provider name from the provisioning namespace.
        /// For instance, "Azure.Provisioning.KeyVault" returns "KeyVault".
        /// </summary>
        protected override string BuildResourceProviderName()
        {
            const string provisioningNamespacePrefix = "Azure.Provisioning.";
            if (PrimaryNamespace.StartsWith(provisioningNamespacePrefix))
            {
                return PrimaryNamespace[provisioningNamespacePrefix.Length..].ToIdentifierName();
            }
            return base.BuildResourceProviderName();
        }

        /// <inheritdoc/>
        protected override CSharpType? CreateCSharpTypeCore(InputType inputType)
        {
            // For model types, check if there's a provisioning-specific type mapping first
            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModel
                && KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputModel.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provisioningType))
            {
                return provisioningType;
            }

            // For enum types, check provisioning mapping too (e.g., ManagedServiceIdentityType)
            if (inputType is InputEnumType inputEnum
                && KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputEnum.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provisioningEnumType))
            {
                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), provisioningEnumType);
            }

            // Let the mgmt base resolve known system types (ResourceIdentifier, AzureLocation, etc.)
            var mgmtType = base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);

            // For model types: if resolved to a system type that's a ProvisionableConstruct, return as-is.
            // Otherwise, for non-ProvisionableConstruct system types (ResponseError from mgmt),
            // wrap in BicepValue<T> since they can't be used with DefineModelProperty.
            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModelType)
            {
                // If base resolution returned null (e.g., model shared by multiple resources),
                // look up the resources directly and use the first resource's type.
                if (mgmtType == null)
                {
                    var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
                    if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(inputModelType, out var sharedResources) && sharedResources.Count > 0)
                    {
                        mgmtType = sharedResources[0].Type;
                    }
                }

                if (mgmtType != null && mgmtType.IsFrameworkType
                    && !typeof(ProvisionableConstruct).IsAssignableFrom(mgmtType.FrameworkType))
                {
                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
                }
                return mgmtType;
            }

            // For enum types, wrap in BicepValue<T>
            // System enums: mgmtType is the system CSharpType
            // Non-system enums: mgmtType is our ProvisioningEnumProvider.Type
            if (inputType is InputEnumType)
            {
                if (mgmtType != null)
                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
                // Fallback: shouldn't happen now that ProvisioningEnumProvider is wired up
                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), typeof(string));
            }

            // For array types, produce BicepList<T> — element type should NOT be BicepValue-wrapped
            if (inputType is InputArrayType arrayType)
            {
                var elementType = GetUnwrappedCSharpType(arrayType.ValueType);
                if (elementType != null)
                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepList<>), elementType);
            }

            // For dictionary types, produce BicepDictionary<TValue> — value type should NOT be BicepValue-wrapped
            if (inputType is InputDictionaryType dictType)
            {
                var valueType = GetUnwrappedCSharpType(dictType.ValueType);
                if (valueType != null)
                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepDictionary<>), valueType);
            }

            // For all other non-model, non-enum types resolved by base (primitives, date/time, duration, etc.),
            // wrap in BicepValue<T>
            if (mgmtType != null)
            {
                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
            }

            return mgmtType;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Resolves an InputType to its raw CSharpType without BicepValue wrapping.
        /// Used for BicepList/BicepDictionary element types which handle wrapping internally.
        /// </summary>
        private CSharpType? GetUnwrappedCSharpType(InputType inputType)
        {
            // For model types, check provisioning mapping first, then fall back to base
            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModel)
            {
                if (KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputModel.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provType))
                    return provType;
                return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType) ?? CreateCSharpType(inputType);
            }

            // For enum types, check provisioning mapping first, then fall back to base
            if (inputType is InputEnumType inputEnum)
            {
                if (KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputEnum.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provEnumType))
                    return provEnumType;
                return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType) ?? typeof(string);
            }

            // For all other types, use the base resolution (returns raw .NET type)
            return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);
        }

        /// <inheritdoc/>
        protected override ModelProvider? CreateModelCore(InputModelType model)
        {
            // Known provisioning types (ManagedServiceIdentity, SystemData, etc.) → null (use framework type)
            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsKnownType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
                return null;

            // Inheritable system types (TrackedResource, ProxyResource, etc.) → null
            // Provisioning types use ProvisionableConstruct/ProvisionableResource as base, not ARM base types
            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsInheritableSystemType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
                return null;

            // "Unknown" discriminator variants are for deserialization fallback in client SDKs.
            // Provisioning types are write-only (compiled to Bicep), so we skip them.
            if (model.IsUnknownDiscriminatorModel)
                return null;

            // Resource models → look up from output library's pre-created resource providers
            var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
            if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(model, out var resources))
            {
                if (resources.Count == 1)
                {
                    return resources[0];
                }
                // Multiple resources share the same model — all resource providers
                // are already added via the Resources list in BuildTypeProviders.
                // Return null here so the model itself is not treated as a resource model,
                // preventing duplicate type generation. For property type resolution,
                // the first resource's type is used (see CreateCSharpTypeCore).
                return null;
            }

            // Derived discriminated resource types → ProvisioningResourceProvider (derived path)
            if (model.DiscriminatorValue != null && IsBaseChainResource(model))
            {
                return new ProvisioningResourceProvider(model);
            }

            // Regular models (including discriminated models) → ProvisioningModelProvider
            return new ProvisioningModelProvider(model);
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Checks whether any model in the base chain is a resource model.
        /// </summary>
        private bool IsBaseChainResource(InputModelType model)
        {
            var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
            var baseModel = model.BaseModel;
            while (baseModel != null)
            {
                if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(baseModel, out _))
                    return true;
                baseModel = baseModel.BaseModel;
            }
            return false;
        }

        /// <inheritdoc/>
        protected override EnumProvider? CreateEnumCore(InputEnumType enumType, TypeProvider? declaringType)
        {
            // Known provisioning enums → null (use framework type)
            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsKnownType(enumType.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
                return null;

            // Regular enums → ProvisioningEnumProvider
            return new ProvisioningEnumProvider(enumType);
        }

        /// <inheritdoc/>
        protected override PropertyProvider? CreatePropertyCore(InputProperty inputProperty, TypeProvider enclosingType)
        {
            // Run base chain which creates property and applies visitor renames (e.g., etag → ETag).
            var baseProperty = base.CreatePropertyCore(inputProperty, enclosingType);

            if (inputProperty is not InputModelProperty inputModelProperty)
                return baseProperty;

            if (enclosingType is IProvisioningPropertyInfo infoProvider)
            {
                var info = infoProvider.GetProvisioningPropertyInfo(inputModelProperty);
                if (info == null) return null;
                var resolvedName = baseProperty?.Name ?? info.PropertyName;
                var bicepType = info.TypeOverride ?? CreateCSharpType(inputModelProperty.Type);
                if (bicepType == null) return null;

                return ProvisioningPropertyProvider.Create(
                    resolvedName, bicepType,
                    info.IsOutput, info.IsRequired, info.BicepPath, info.DefaultValue,
                    enclosingType);
            }

            return baseProperty;
        }
    }
}

   115	            }
   116	
   117	            return mgmtType;
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        /// <summary>
   121	        /// Resolves an InputType to its raw CSharpType without BicepValue wrapping.
   122	        /// Used for BicepList/BicepDictionary element types which handle wrapping internally.
   123	        /// </summary>
   124	        private CSharpType? GetUnwrappedCSharpType(InputType inputType)
   125	        {
   126	            // For model types, check provisioning mapping first, then fall back to base
   127	            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModel)
   128	            {
   129	                if (KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputModel.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provType))
   130	                    return provType;
   131	                return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType) ?? CreateCSharpType(inputType);
   132	            }
   133	
   134	            // For enum types, check provisioning mapping first, then fall back to base
   135	            if (inputType is InputEnumType inputEnum)
   136	            {
   137	                if (KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputEnum.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provEnumType))
   138	                    return provEnumType;
   139	                return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType) ?? typeof(string);
   140	            }
   141	
   142	            // For all other types, use the base resolution (returns raw .NET type)
   143	            return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   147	        protected override ModelProvider? CreateModelCore(InputModelType model)
   148	        {
   149	            // Known provisioning types (ManagedServiceIdentity, SystemData, etc.) → null (use framework type)
   150	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsKnownType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   151	                return null;
   152	
   153	            // Inheritable system types (TrackedResource, ProxyResource, etc.) → null
   154	            // Provisioning types use ProvisionableConstruct/ProvisionableResource as base, not ARM base types
   155	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsInheritableSystemType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   156	                return null;
   157	
   158	            // "Unknown" discriminator variants are for deserialization fallback in client SDKs.
   159	            // Provisioning types are write-only (compiled to Bicep), so we skip them.
   160	            if (model.IsUnknownDiscriminatorModel)
   161	                return null;
   162	
   163	            // Resource models → look up from output library's pre-created resource providers
   164	            var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
   165	            if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(model, out var resources))
   166	            {
   167	                if (resources.Count == 1)
   168	                {
   169	                    return resources[0];
   170	                }
   171	                // Multiple resources share the same model — all resource providers
   172	                // are already added via the Resources list in BuildTypeProviders.
   173	                // Return null here so the model itself is not treated as a resource model,
   174	                // preventing duplicate type generation. For property type resolution,
   175	                // the first resource's type is used (see CreateCSharpTypeCore).
   176	                return null;
   177	            }
   178	
   179	            // Derived discriminated resource types → ProvisioningResourceProvider (derived path)
   180	            if (model.DiscriminatorValue != null && IsBaseChainResource(model))
   181	            {
   182	                return new ProvisioningResourceProvider(model);
   183	            }
   184	
   185	            // Regular models (including discriminated models) → ProvisioningModelProvider
   186	            return new ProvisioningModelProvider(model);
   187	        }
   188	
   189	        /// <summary>
   190	        /// Checks whether any model in the base chain is a resource model.
   191	        /// </summary>
   192	        private bool IsBaseChainResource(InputModelType model)
   193	        {
   194	            var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
   195	            var baseModel = model.BaseModel;
   196	            while (baseModel != null)
   197	            {
   198	                if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(baseModel, out _))
   199	                    return true;
   200	                baseModel = baseModel.BaseModel;
   201	            }
   202	            return false;
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   206	        protected override EnumProvider? CreateEnumCore(InputEnumType enumType, TypeProvider? declaringType)
   207	        {
   208	            // Known provisioning enums → null (use framework type)
   209	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsKnownType(enumType.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   210	                return null;
   211	
   212	            // Regular enums → ProvisioningEnumProvider
   213	            return new ProvisioningEnumProvider(enumType);
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   217	        protected override PropertyProvider? CreatePropertyCore(InputProperty inputProperty, TypeProvider enclosingType)
   218	        {
   219	            // Run base chain which creates property and applies visitor renames (e.g., etag → ETag).
   220	            var baseProperty = base.CreatePropertyCore(inputProperty, enclosingType);
   221	
   222	            if (inputProperty is not InputModelProperty inputModelProperty)
   223	                return baseProperty;
   224	
   225	            if (enclosingType is IProvisioningPropertyInfo infoProvider)
   226	            {
   227	                var info = infoProvider.GetProvisioningPropertyInfo(inputModelProperty);
   228	                if (info == null) return null;
   229	                var resolvedName = baseProperty?.Name ?? info.PropertyName;
   230	                var bicepType = info.TypeOverride ?? CreateCSharpType(inputModelProperty.Type);
   231	                if (bicepType == null) return null;
   232	
   233	                return ProvisioningPropertyProvider.Create(
   234	                    resolvedName, bicepType,
   235	                    info.IsOutput, info.IsRequired, info.BicepPath, info.DefaultValue,
   236	                    enclosingType);
   237	            }
   238	
   239	            return baseProperty;
   240	        }
   241	    }
   242	}

    13	/// <summary>
    14	/// Visitor that removes the "Data" suffix from resource model names.
    15	/// The mgmt ResourceVisitor appends "Data" to resource models (e.g., ConfigurationStore → ConfigurationStoreData).
    16	/// Provisioning libraries do not use the "Data" suffix (e.g., AppConfigurationStore, not AppConfigurationStoreData).
    17	/// This visitor runs after the inherited mgmt visitors and reverts the rename.
    18	/// </summary>
    19	internal class ResourceDataSuffixVisitor : ScmLibraryVisitor
    20	{
    21	    private const string DataSuffix = "Data";
    22	
    23	    protected override ModelProvider? PreVisitModel(InputModelType model, ModelProvider? type)
    24	    {
    25	        if (type is not null && ((ManagementInputLibrary)ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.InputLibrary).IsResourceModel(model))
    26	        {
    27	            var name = type.Name;
    28	            if (name.EndsWith(DataSuffix, StringComparison.Ordinal))
    29	            {
    30	                var originalName = name.Substring(0, name.Length - DataSuffix.Length);
    31	                type.Update(
    32	                    name: originalName,
    33	                    relativeFilePath: Path.Combine("src", "Generated", $"{originalName}.cs"));
    34	            }
    35	        }
    36	        return type;
    37	    }
    38	}

```csharp
    }
```

`base.CreateCSharpTypeCore` → `ManagementTypeFactory.CreateCSharpTypeCore` → calls `CreateModel` → `CreateModelCore` returns null for multi-resource → returns null. Then falls back to `CreateCSharpType(inputType)` → `CreateCSharpTypeCore` (our override) → has multi-resource fallback → returns `sharedResources[0].Type`.

But wait, `CreateCSharpType` calls `CreateCSharpTypeCore` which then calls `base.CreateCSharpTypeCore` again... that would be a recursive loop? No, let me check:

`CreateCSharpType` is defined in the base class. It probably does:
```csharp
public CSharpType? CreateCSharpType(InputType inputType) => CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);
```

So `CreateCSharpType` calls our overridden `CreateCSharpTypeCore`. In our override, we call `base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType)` which calls `ManagementTypeFactory.CreateCSharpTypeCore` → ... → `CreateModel` → `CreateModelCore` returns null (cached or not). So the flow for `GetUnwrappedCSharpType`:
1. `base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType)` → eventually calls `CreateModel` → returns null (cached) → `base.CreateCSharpTypeCore` returns null
2. Falls back to `CreateCSharpType(inputType)` → calls `CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType)` (our override)
3. Our override: calls `base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType)` → returns null (same as step 1)
4. `mgmtType` is null, hits our new fallback: queries resources directly, gets `sharedResources[0].Type`
5. Returns that type (a model type, not a framework type, not wrapped)

This should work correctly.

```csharp
private bool IsBaseChainResource(InputModelType model)
{
    var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
    var baseModel = model.BaseModel;
    while (baseModel != null)
    {
        if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(baseModel, out _))
            return true;
        baseModel = baseModel.BaseModel;
    }
    return false;
}
```

     1	// Copyright (c) Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.

     4	using Azure.Generator.Management;
     5	using Azure.Generator.Provisioning.Primitives;
     6	using Azure.Generator.Provisioning.Providers;
     7	using Azure.Provisioning;
     8	using Azure.Provisioning.Primitives;
     9	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Input;
    10	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Input.Extensions;
    11	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Primitives;
    12	using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Providers;
    13	using System;
    14	using System.Linq;
    15	
    16	namespace Azure.Generator.Provisioning
    17	{
    18	    /// <summary>
    19	    /// TypeFactory for provisioning generator that intercepts model/enum creation
    20	    /// to return provisioning-style type providers (ProvisionableConstruct/ProvisionableResource)
    21	    /// instead of management-style types.
    22	    /// </summary>
    23	    public class ProvisioningTypeFactory : ManagementTypeFactory
    24	    {
    25	        /// <summary>
    26	        /// Builds the resource provider name from the provisioning namespace.
    27	        /// For instance, "Azure.Provisioning.KeyVault" returns "KeyVault".
    28	        /// </summary>
    29	        protected override string BuildResourceProviderName()
    30	        {
    31	            const string provisioningNamespacePrefix = "Azure.Provisioning.";
    32	            if (PrimaryNamespace.StartsWith(provisioningNamespacePrefix))
    33	            {
    34	                return PrimaryNamespace[provisioningNamespacePrefix.Length..].ToIdentifierName();
    35	            }
    36	            return base.BuildResourceProviderName();
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        /// <inheritdoc/>
    40	        protected override CSharpType? CreateCSharpTypeCore(InputType inputType)
    41	        {
    42	            // For model types, check if there's a provisioning-specific type mapping first
    43	            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModel
    44	                && KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputModel.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provisioningType))
    45	            {
    46	                return provisioningType;
    47	            }
    48	
    49	            // For enum types, check provisioning mapping too (e.g., ManagedServiceIdentityType)
    50	            if (inputType is InputEnumType inputEnum
    51	                && KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputEnum.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provisioningEnumType))
    52	            {
    53	                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), provisioningEnumType);
    54	            }
    55	
    56	            // Let the mgmt base resolve known system types (ResourceIdentifier, AzureLocation, etc.)
    57	            var mgmtType = base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);
    58	
    59	            // For model types: if resolved to a system type that's a ProvisionableConstruct, return as-is.
    60	            // Otherwise, for non-ProvisionableConstruct system types (ResponseError from mgmt),
    61	            // wrap in BicepValue<T> since they can't be used with DefineModelProperty.
    62	            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModelType)
    63	            {
    64	                // If base resolution returned null (e.g., model shared by multiple resources),
    65	                // look up the resources directly and use the first resource's type.
    66	                if (mgmtType == null)
    67	                {
    68	                    var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
    69	                    if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(inputModelType, out var sharedResources) && sharedResources.Count > 0)
    70	                    {
    71	                        mgmtType = sharedResources[0].Type;
    72	                    }
    73	                }
    74	
    75	                if (mgmtType != null && mgmtType.IsFrameworkType
    76	                    && !typeof(ProvisionableConstruct).IsAssignableFrom(mgmtType.FrameworkType))
    77	                {
    78	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
    79	                }
    80	                return mgmtType;
    81	            }
    82	
    83	            // For enum types, wrap in BicepValue<T>
    84	            // System enums: mgmtType is the system CSharpType
    85	            // Non-system enums: mgmtType is our ProvisioningEnumProvider.Type
    86	            if (inputType is InputEnumType)
    87	            {
    88	                if (mgmtType != null)
    89	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
    90	                // Fallback: shouldn't happen now that ProvisioningEnumProvider is wired up
    91	                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), typeof(string));
    92	            }
    93	
    94	            // For array types, produce BicepList<T> — element type should NOT be BicepValue-wrapped
    95	            if (inputType is InputArrayType arrayType)
    96	            {
    97	                var elementType = GetUnwrappedCSharpType(arrayType.ValueType);
    98	                if (elementType != null)
    99	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepList<>), elementType);
   100	            }
   101	
   102	            // For dictionary types, produce BicepDictionary<TValue> — value type should NOT be BicepValue-wrapped
   103	            if (inputType is InputDictionaryType dictType)
   104	            {
   105	                var valueType = GetUnwrappedCSharpType(dictType.ValueType);
   106	                if (valueType != null)
   107	                    return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepDictionary<>), valueType);
   108	            }
   109	
   110	            // For all other non-model, non-enum types resolved by base (primitives, date/time, duration, etc.),
   111	            // wrap in BicepValue<T>
   112	            if (mgmtType != null)
   113	            {
   114	                return new CSharpType(typeof(BicepValue<>), mgmtType);
   115	            }
   116	
   117	            return mgmtType;
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        /// <summary>
   121	        /// Resolves an InputType to its raw CSharpType without BicepValue wrapping.
   122	        /// Used for BicepList/BicepDictionary element types which handle wrapping internally.
   123	        /// </summary>
   124	        private CSharpType? GetUnwrappedCSharpType(InputType inputType)
   125	        {
   126	            // For model types, check provisioning mapping first, then fall back to base
   127	            if (inputType is InputModelType inputModel)
   128	            {
   129	                if (KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputModel.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provType))
   130	                    return provType;
   131	                return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType) ?? CreateCSharpType(inputType);
   132	            }
   133	
   134	            // For enum types, check provisioning mapping first, then fall back to base
   135	            if (inputType is InputEnumType inputEnum)
   136	            {
   137	                if (KnownProvisioningTypes.TryGetProvisioningType(inputEnum.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var provEnumType))
   138	                    return provEnumType;
   139	                return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType) ?? typeof(string);
   140	            }
   141	
   142	            // For all other types, use the base resolution (returns raw .NET type)
   143	            return base.CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   147	        protected override ModelProvider? CreateModelCore(InputModelType model)
   148	        {
   149	            // Known provisioning types (ManagedServiceIdentity, SystemData, etc.) → null (use framework type)
   150	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsKnownType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   151	                return null;
   152	
   153	            // Inheritable system types (TrackedResource, ProxyResource, etc.) → null
   154	            // Provisioning types use ProvisionableConstruct/ProvisionableResource as base, not ARM base types
   155	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsInheritableSystemType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   156	                return null;
   157	
   158	            // "Unknown" discriminator variants are for deserialization fallback in client SDKs.
   159	            // Provisioning types are write-only (compiled to Bicep), so we skip them.
   160	            if (model.IsUnknownDiscriminatorModel)
   161	                return null;
   162	
   163	            // Resource models → look up from output library's pre-created resource providers
   164	            var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
   165	            if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(model, out var resources))
   166	            {
   167	                if (resources.Count == 1)
   168	                {
   169	                    return resources[0];
   170	                }
   171	                // Multiple resources share the same model — all resource providers
   172	                // are already added via the Resources list in BuildTypeProviders.
   173	                // Return null here so the model itself is not treated as a resource model,
   174	                // preventing duplicate type generation. For property type resolution,
   175	                // the first resource's type is used (see CreateCSharpTypeCore).
   176	                return null;
   177	            }
   178	
   179	            // Derived discriminated resource types → ProvisioningResourceProvider (derived path)
   180	            if (model.DiscriminatorValue != null && IsBaseChainResource(model))
   181	            {
   182	                return new ProvisioningResourceProvider(model);
   183	            }
   184	
   185	            // Regular models (including discriminated models) → ProvisioningModelProvider
   186	            return new ProvisioningModelProvider(model);
   187	        }
   188	
   189	        /// <summary>
   190	        /// Checks whether any model in the base chain is a resource model.
   191	        /// </summary>
   192	        private bool IsBaseChainResource(InputModelType model)
   193	        {
   194	            var outputLib = ProvisioningGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary;
   195	            var baseModel = model.BaseModel;
   196	            while (baseModel != null)
   197	            {
   198	                if (outputLib.TryGetResourcesByModel(baseModel, out _))
   199	                    return true;
   200	                baseModel = baseModel.BaseModel;
   201	            }
   202	            return false;
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   206	        protected override EnumProvider? CreateEnumCore(InputEnumType enumType, TypeProvider? declaringType)
   207	        {
   208	            // Known provisioning enums → null (use framework type)
   209	            if (KnownProvisioningTypes.IsKnownType(enumType.CrossLanguageDefinitionId))
   210	                return null;
   211	
   212	            // Regular enums → ProvisioningEnumProvider
   213	            return new ProvisioningEnumProvider(enumType);
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   217	        protected override PropertyProvider? CreatePropertyCore(InputProperty inputProperty, TypeProvider enclosingType)
   218	        {
   219	            // Run base chain which creates property and applies visitor renames (e.g., etag → ETag).
   220	            var baseProperty = base.CreatePropertyCore(inputProperty, enclosingType);
   221	
   222	            if (inputProperty is not InputModelProperty inputModelProperty)
   223	                return baseProperty;
   224	
   225	            if (enclosingType is IProvisioningPropertyInfo infoProvider)
   226	            {
   227	                var info = infoProvider.GetProvisioningPropertyInfo(inputModelProperty);
   228	                if (info == null) return null;
   229	                var resolvedName = baseProperty?.Name ?? info.PropertyName;
   230	                var bicepType = info.TypeOverride ?? CreateCSharpType(inputModelProperty.Type);
   231	                if (bicepType == null) return null;
   232	
   233	                return ProvisioningPropertyProvider.Create(
   234	                    resolvedName, bicepType,
   235	                    info.IsOutput, info.IsRequired, info.BicepPath, info.DefaultValue,
   236	                    enclosingType);
   237	            }
   238	
   239	            return baseProperty;
   240	        }
   241	    }
   242	}

For property type resolution, this might be confusing (which resource is the "correct" one?). CreateCSharpType(InputType inputType) => CreateCSharpTypeCore(inputType);\n```\n\nSo it\'s just a public wrapper. The caching happens at the `CreateModel` level. Let me summarize what was done:\n\n## Summary of Changes\n\n### Problem\nThe `ProvisioningTypeFactory.CreateModelCore` method assumed one resource model maps to exactly one resource definition. When multiple ARM resources share the same resource model (which happens in some management RPs), it threw a `NotSupportedException`. Additionally, when other models reference a resource model as a property type and that model is shared across multiple resources, it was unclear which resource class to use.\n\n### Changes Made\n\n**1. `ProvisioningTypeFactory.cs` - `CreateModelCore` method (lines 171-176)**\n- Replaced the `NotSupportedException` throw with `return null`\n- When multiple resources share the same model, the method now returns `null` instead of throwing\n- All resource providers are already generated from the `Resources` list in `BuildTypeProviders`, so we don\'t need to return one here\n- Updated the comment to explain the reasoning\n\n**2. `ProvisioningTypeFactory.cs` - `CreateCSharpTypeCore` method (lines 62-74)**\n- Changed `if (inputType is InputModelType)` to `if (inputType is InputModelType inputModelType)` to capture the typed variable\n- Added a fallback: when `base.CreateCSharpTypeCore` returns `null` (which happens when `CreateModelCore` returns `null` for multi-resource models), the code now directly looks up resources from the output library and uses the first resource\'s type\n- This ensures property type resolution works correctly for models shared by multiple resources\n\n**3. `design.md` - Type Resolution Flow section**\n- Updated the documentation to reflect the new behavior:\n  - Split "ARM resource model?" into "ARM resource model (single)?" and "ARM resource model (multiple)?"\n  - Added note about multi-resource model type resolution using the first resource\'s type as fallback', role='assistant', tool_calls=None, function_call=None, provider_specific_fields={'refusal': None}), provider_specific_fields={'content_filter_results': {}})], usage=Usage(completion_tokens=407, prompt_tokens=89484, total_tokens=89891, completion_tokens_details=None, prompt_tokens_details=None, audio_prompt_tokens=0), service_tier=None, prompt_filter_results=None)
